==> Codex issue attempt 1
Codex execution started; transcript output is excluded from persisted run logs.
Codex execution completed.
Codex final message:
Implemented the password-hash verification abstraction in [hushline/password_hasher.py]([redacted-path] and routed [User.check_password]([redacted-path] through it. The new module does explicit prefix dispatch: `$scrypt$` goes to legacy passlib verification, `prefix:` hashes go through the new primary verifier path, unknown prefixes fail closed, and every verification emits structured aggregate telemetry with only `hash_format`/`hash_prefix` labels.

Added focused coverage in [tests/test_password_hasher.py]([redacted-path] for legacy success, native-prefix dispatch, unknown-prefix fail-closed behavior, malformed legacy hashes, and the absence of usernames/passwords/raw hashes in telemetry. I also tightened [tests/test_registration_and_login.py]([redacted-path] so registration still proves it writes passlib scrypt hashes.

I did not run local validation. The pre-existing unrelated change in [hushline/static/js/directory_verified.js]([redacted-path] was left untouched.
